    SELECT TOP(2) [a].[Id], [a].[Address], [a].[AttractionTypes], [a].[Author], [a].[AuthorId], [a].[AvgRates], [a].[Contact], [a].[CreateDate], [a].[Currency], [a].[DefaultExperienceId], [a].[DefaultGalleryId], [a].[DefaultName], [a].[Description], [a].[DestinationId], [a].[FromExperience], [a].[Latitude], [a].[Longitude], [a].[MapImageUri], [a].[PriceFrom], [a].[Priority], [a].[PropertyGroups], [a].[RouteUri], [a].[Status], [a].[ThumbnailUrl], [a].[TotalComments], [a].[TotalLikes], [a].[TotalRates], [a].[TouristClasses], [a].[TouristObjects], [a].[VisitDuration], [a].[Website], [d].[Id] AS [Id0], [d].[AvgRates] AS [AvgRates0], [d].[BannerUrl], [d].[CityId], [d].[CityName], [d].[Continent], [d].[CountryId], [d].[CountryName], [d].[DefaultGalleryId] AS [DefaultGalleryId0], [d].[DefaultName] AS [DefaultName0], [d].[Description] AS [Description0], [d].[DestinationOverviewId], [d].[Latitude] AS [Latitude0], [d].[Longitude] AS [Longitude0], [d].[MapImageUri] AS [MapImageUri0], [d].[RouteUri] AS [RouteUri0], [d].[StateId], [d].[StateName], [d].[ThumbnailUrl] AS [ThumbnailUrl0], [d].[TotalLikes] AS [TotalLikes0], [d].[TotalRates] AS [TotalRates0]
